The `public contributions` and `private contributions` by users in Georgia on `2024/12/19 4:25 AM UTC`. This list contains users from `Georgia` and cities `Tbilisi` `Batumi` `Kutaisi` `Rustavi`.

There are `137 countries` and `666 cities` can be found [here](https://github.com/Zaid-maker/top-github-users-list).

There are `969 users`  in Georgia. You need at least `18 followers` to be on this list.

## üì¶ Third party

- [@octokit/graphql](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@octokit/graphql) - Send GraphQL requests to GitHub API.
- [fs-extra](https://www.npmjs.com/package/fs-extra) - Creating directories and files.
- [simple-git](https://www.npmjs.com/package/simple-git) - Handling Git commands.
